Node API - Osmosis Tendermint RPC

Authenticationâ€‹

API calls require authentication with API key via Authorization request header or URL property. Calls are made to the Osmosis Tendermint Rpc Node API endpoint, hosted at https://osmosis-1--rpc--archive.datahub.figment.io

Here's some boilerplate to get you started.
  • Fetch with Header
  • Fetch with Parameter
  • CURL with Header
  • CURL with Parameter
fetch("https://osmosis-1--rpc--archive.datahub.figment.io/", {
    method: 'POST', // can also be 'GET', 'PUT' or any appropriate method
    headers: {
        "Authorization" : "<api_key>",
        "Content-Type": "application/json" // if method is 'POST'
    },
    body: JSON.stringify({
      // JSON Payload
    })
})
fetch("https://osmosis-1--rpc--archive.datahub.figment.io/apikey/<api_key>/", {
    method: 'POST', // can also be 'GET', 'PUT' or any appropriate method
    headers: {
        "Content-Type": "application/json" // if method is 'POST'
    },
    body: JSON.stringify({
      // JSON Payload
    })
})
curl -X POST 'https://osmosis-1--rpc--archive.datahub.figment.io/' \
--header 'Content-Type: application/json' \
--header 'Authorization: <api_key>' \
--data '{
  // JSON Payload
}'
curl -X POST 'https://osmosis-1--rpc--archive.datahub.figment.io/apikey/<api_key>/' \
--header 'Content-Type: application/json' \
--data '{
  // JSON Payload
}'

Available Methods

/health

Get node health.

View specification

Parameters

  • None

Response

  • On success, returns an empty result: (200 OK)
  • On error, no response is returned.
Request Query (try it)
/health
Example Response
{
  "jsonrpc": "2.0",
  "id": -1,
  "result": {}
}

/status

Get tendermint status including node info, pubkey, latest block hash, app hash, block height, and time.

View specification

Parameters

  • None

Response

  • Returns tendermint status including node_info, sync_info, validator_info pubkey, latest block hash, app hash, block height, and time.
Request Query (try it)
/status
Example Response
{
  "jsonrpc": "2.0",
  "id": -1,
  "result": {
    "node_info": {
      "protocol_version": {
        "p2p": "8",
        "block": "11",
        "app": "10"
      },
      "id": "e17d17450f50ee0c7052a730cbbab098de4e4d2d",
      "listen_addr": "tcp://15.235.53.174:26656",
      "network": "osmosis-1",
      "version": "0.34.19",
      "channels": "40202122233038606100",
      "moniker": "F7SGAlNtKb",
      "other": {
        "tx_index": "on",
        "rpc_address": "tcp://0.0.0.0:26657"
      }
    },
    "sync_info": {
      "latest_block_hash": "1C9A053FAFD52AB9A52B0FC35F6F0AEC1C41A9B317FD794A327802013CF353D0",
      "latest_app_hash": "A85A1D805BC0E0F8B47EA590A8D3B154D14F9D92EA9FCBCE473F99D4657EBF6B",
      "latest_block_height": "5748134",
      "latest_block_time": "2022-08-26T08:23:46.992977879Z",
      "earliest_block_hash": "C8DC787FAAE0941EF05C75C3AECCF04B85DFB1D4A8D054A463F323B0D9459719",
      "earliest_app_hash": "E3B0C44298FC1C149AFBF4C8996FB92427AE41E4649B934CA495991B7852B855",
      "earliest_block_height": "1",
      "earliest_block_time": "2021-06-18T17:00:00Z",
      "catching_up": false
    },
    "validator_info": {
      "address": "942B28577FFC30E9044DE6823ED7B819B18FA635",
      "pub_key": {
        "type": "tendermint/PubKeyEd25519",
        "value": "8Z6138Lc3x1xogZoJyZh8g7Hu1Ja1+XapMwkUmnOAoY="
      },
      "voting_power": "0"
    }
  }
}

/blockchain

Get block headers for minHeight <= height maxHeight.

View specification

At most 20 items will be returned.

Parameters

  • minHeight integer (query) - Minimum block height to return.
  • maxHeight integer (query) - Maximum block height to return

Response

  • Returns block headers for the given height params.
Request Query (try it)
/blockchain?minHeight=5748240&maxHeight=5748241
Example Response
{

/block

Get block at a specified height

View specification

Parameters

  • height integer (query) - height to return. If no height is provided, it will fetch the latest block.

Response

  • Returns the block from the specified height. If no height is provided, it returns the latest block.
Request Query (try it)
/block?height=5748241
Example Response
{
  "jsonrpc": "2.0",
  "id": -1,
  "result": {
    "block_id": {
      "hash": "8E22FD04F8367A13476F5FB78D7986EF6699FA1DB70ABD1D10B11E3E70265FD7",

/block_by_hash

Get Block By Hash.

View specification

Parameters

  • hash string (query) - block hash (add 0x with block hash)

Response

  • Returns the block details for the given hash.
Request Query (try it)
/block_by_hash?hash=0x8E22FD04F8367A13476F5FB78D7986EF6699FA1DB70ABD1D10B11E3E70265FD7

/block_Response

Get block Response at a specified height.

View specification

Parameters

  • height integer (query) - height to return. If no height is provided, it will fetch informations regarding the latest block. Default value : 0

Response

  • height height provided to query the block Response.
  • txs_Response block Response
Request Query (try it)
/block_Response?height=5748241

/commit

Get commit Response at a specified height.

View specification

Parameters

  • height integer (query) - height to return. If no height is provided, it will fetch informations regarding the latest block. Default value : 0

Response

  • Commit Response, canonical switches from false to true for block H once block H+1 has been committed. Until then it's subjective and only reflects what this node has seen so far.
Request Query (try it)
/commit?height=5748241
Example Response
{
  "jsonrpc": "2.0",
  "id": -1,
  "result": {
    "signed_header": {
      "header": {
        "version": {
          "block": "11",
          "app": "10"
        },
        "chain_id": "osmosis-1",
        "height": "5748241",
        "time": "2022-08-26T08:34:44.600390862Z",
        "last_block_id": {
          "hash": "42D3EC90D59AB536766D9C61CD2DFA1B9E330B5466D4D72D861AB8C4EB5CC4FD",
          "parts": {
            "total": 2,
            "hash": "36ABB6012BC5A4C926CFE25AD94089BE96170170F072D134C6755A6A62D9E525"
          }
        },

/validators

Get validators set at a specified height. Validators are sorted by voting power.

View specification

Parameters

  • height integer (query) - height to return. If no height is provided, it will fetch validator set which corresponds to the latest block. Default value : 0
  • page integer (query) - Page number (1-based). Default value : 1
  • per_page integer (query) Number of entries per page (max: 100). Default value : 30

Response

  • Returns the validator set for the given height
Request Query (try it)
/validators?height=5748241
Example Response
{
  "jsonrpc": "2.0",
  "id": -1,
  "result": {
    "block_height": "5748241",
    "validators": [
      {
        "address": "CB5A63B91E8F4EE8DB935942CBE25724636479E0",
        "pub_key": {
          "type": "tendermint/PubKeyEd25519",
          "value": "6Nz09YGHzwWxjczG0IhK4Iv0qY2IcX0P/5KitvRXTUc="
        },
        "voting_power": "20401886",
        "proposer_priority": "-72523380"
      }
    ],
    "count": "30",
    "total": "135"
  }
}

/dump_consensus_state

Get consensus state.

View specification

Not safe to call from inside the ABCI application during a block execution.

Parameters

  • None

Response

  • Returns complete consensus state. See https://pkg.go.dev/github.com/tendermint/tendermint/types?tab=doc#Vote.String for Vote string description.

/dump_consensus_state

/consensus_params

Get consensus parameters.

View specification

Parameters

  • height integer (query) - height to return. If no height is provided, it will fetch commit informations regarding the latest block. Default value : 0

Response

  • Returns block_height and consensus_params
Request Query (try it)
/consensus_params?height=5748241
Example Response
{
  "jsonrpc": "2.0",
  "id": -1,
  "result": {
    "block_height": "5748241",
    "consensus_params": {
      "block": {
        "max_bytes": "10485760",
        "max_gas": "120000000",
        "time_iota_ms": "1000"
      },
      "evidence": {
        "max_age_num_blocks": "403200",
        "max_age_duration": "1209600000000000",
        "max_bytes": "1048576"
      },
      "validator": {
        "pub_key_types": [
          "ed25519"
        ]
      },
      "version": {
        "app_version": "10"
      }
    }
  }
}

/unconfirmed_txs

View specification

Parameters

  • limit integer (query) - Maximum number of unconfirmed transactions to return (max 100) Default value : 30

  • Returns list of unconfirmed transactions

/num_unconfirmed_txs

Get data about unconfirmed transactions

View specification

Parameters

  • None

Response

  • Returns the totals number of unconfirmed transactions.
Request Query (try it)
/num_unconfirmed_txs
Example Response
{
  "jsonrpc": "2.0",
  "id": -1,
  "result": {
    "n_txs": "3",
    "total": "3",
    "total_bytes": "1325",
    "txs": null
  }
}

/tx_search

Search for transactions w/ their Response.

View specification

Parameters

  • query string (query) (required) - Query (ex. tx.height=1000)
  • prove boolean (query) - Include proofs of the transactions inclusion in the block. Default value : false
  • page integer (query) - Page number (1-based). Default value : 1
  • per_page integer (query) - Number of entries per page (max: 100). Default value : 30
  • order_by string (query) - Order in which transactions are sorted ("asc" or "desc"), by height & index. If empty, default sorting will be still applied. Default value : asc

Response

  • Returns the transactions specified by the given parameters.
Request Query (try it)
/tx_search?query=%22tx.height%3D5748241%22

/block_search

Search for blocks by BeginBlock and EndBlock events.

View specification

Parameters

  • query string (query) (required) - Query (ex. block.height > 1000 AND valset.changed > 0)
  • page integer (query) - Page number (1-based). Default value : 1
  • per_page integer (query) - Number of entries per page (max: 100). Default value : 30
  • order_by string (query) - Order in which transactions are sorted ("asc" or "desc"), by height & index. If empty, default sorting will be still applied. Default value : asc

Response

  • Returns the specified transaction on given params.
Request Query (try it)
/block_search?query=%22block.height%3D5748241%22

/tx

Get transactions by hash.

View specification

Parameters

  • hash string (query) (required) - transaction Hash to retrive
  • prove boolean (query) Include proofs of the transactions inclusion in the block. Default value : false

Response

  • Returns details of the transaction for the given hash.
Request Query (try it)
/tx?hash=0x26EA8220BEC3571E777276148B221446836D7A0D13F6EBC547C4E457EA450AC7
Example Response
{
  "jsonrpc": "2.0",
  "id": -1,
  "result": {
    "hash": "26EA8220BEC3571E777276148B221446836D7A0D13F6EBC547C4E457EA450AC7",
    "height": "5748241",
    "index": 0,
    "tx_result": {
      "code": 0,

/broadcast_evidence

Broadcast evidence of the misbehavior.

View specification

Parameters

  • evidence string (query) JSON evidence

Response

  • Returns the confirmation of broadcasted evidence of misbehavior.
Request Query (try it)
/broadcast_evidence?evidence=JSON_EVIDENCE_encoded
Example Response
{
  "jsonrpc": "2.0",
  "id": -1,
  "error": {
    "code": -32603,
    "message": "Internal error",
    "data": "no evidence was provided"
  }
}

/broadcast_tx_sync

Returns with the response from CheckTx. Does not wait for DeliverTx result.

View specification

Parameters

  • tx string (query) (required) The transaction

Response

  • Returns transaction response from CheckTx.
Request Query (try it)
/broadcast_tx_sync?tx=456
Example Response
{
  "jsonrpc": "2.0",
  "id": 0,
  "result": {
    "code": "0",
    "data": "",
    "log": "",
    "codespace": "ibc",
    "hash": "0D33F2F03A5234F38706E43004489E061AC40A2E"
  },
  "error": ""
}

/broadcast_tx_async

Returns right away, with no response. Does not wait for CheckTx nor DeliverTx Response.

View specification

Parameters

  • tx string (query) (required) The transaction

Response

  • Returns transaction response
Request Query (try it)
/broadcast_tx_async?tx=123
Example Response
{
  "jsonrpc": "2.0",
  "id": 0,
  "result": {
    "code": "0",
    "data": "",
    "log": "",
    "codespace": "ibc",
    "hash": "0D33F2F03A5234F38706E43004489E061AC40A2E"
  },
  "error": ""
}

/broadcast_tx_commit

Returns with the responses from CheckTx and DeliverTx.

View specification

Parameters

  • tx string (query) (required) The transaction

Response

  • Returns transaction response from CheckTx and DeliverTx.
Request Query (try it)
/broadcast_tx_commit?tx=785
Example Response
{
  "error": "",
  "result": {
    "height": "26682",
    "hash": "75CA0F856A4DA078FC4911580360E70CEFB2EBEE",
    "deliver_tx": {
      "log": "",
      "data": "",
      "code": "0"
    },
    "check_tx": {
      "log": "",
      "data": "",
      "code": "0"
    }
  },
  "id": 0,
  "jsonrpc": "2.0"
}

/check_tx

Checks the transaction without executing it.

View specification

The transaction won't be added to the mempool.

Parameters

  • tx string (query) (required) The transaction

Response

  • Returns checked transaction response.
Request Query (try it)
/check_tx?tx=785
Example Response
{
  "error": "",
  "result": {
    "code": "0",
    "data": "",
    "log": "",
    "info": "",
    "gas_wanted": "1",
    "gas_used": "0",
    "events": [
      {
        "type": "app",
        "attributes": [
          {
            "key": "YWN0aW9u",
            "value": "c2VuZA==",
            "index": false
          }
        ]
      }
    ],
    "codespace": "bank"
  },
  "id": 0,
  "jsonrpc": "2.0"
}

/abci_info

Get some info about the application.

View specification

Parameters

  • None

Response

  • Returns application info which includes data, version, last_block_height and last_block_app_hash.
Request Query (try it)
/abci_info
Example Response
{
  "jsonrpc": "2.0",
  "id": -1,
  "result": {
    "response": {
      "data": "OsmosisApp",
      "version": "11.0.1",
      "app_version": "10",
      "last_block_height": "5748792",
      "last_block_app_hash": "6nX/XRk8rsmtix7uLdDroJjjdTfnx9MmAi9Ufg6TnWc="
    }
  }
}

/abci_query

Query the application for some information.

View specification

Parameters

  • path string (query) (required) Path to the data ("/a/b/c").
  • data string (query) (required) Data
  • height integer (query) Height (0 means latest). Default value : 0
  • prove boolean (query) Include proofs of the transactions inclusion in the block. Default value : false

Response

  • Returns the information for the given application.
Request Query (try it)
/abci_query?path=%22/app/version%22&data&height=0&prove=true
Example Response
{
  "jsonrpc": "2.0",
  "id": -1,
  "result": {
    "response": {
      "code": 0,
      "log": "",
      "info": "",
      "index": "0",
      "key": null,
      "value": "MTEuMC4x",
      "proofOps": null,
      "height": "5748795",
      "codespace": "sdk"
    }
  }
}
